The connection manager bases further\\n36:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\\n37:  */\\n38: enum class FilterHeadersStatus {\\n39:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\\n40:   Continue,\\n41:   // Do not iterate for headers on any of the remaining filters in the chain.\\n42:   //\\n43:   // Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\\n44:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n45:   //\\n46:   // Note that if a local reply was sent, no further iteration for headers as well as data and\\n47:   // trailers for the current filter and the filters following will happen. A local reply can be\\n48:   // triggered via sendLocalReply() or encodeHeaders().\\n49:   StopIteration,\\n50:   // Continue headers iteration to remaining filters, but delay ending the stream. This status MUST\\n51:   // NOT be returned when end_stream is already set to false.\\n52:   //\\n53:   // Used when a filter wants to add a body to a headers-only request/response, but this body is not\\n54:   // readily available. Delaying end_stream allows the filter to add the body once it's available\\n55:   // without stopping headers iteration.\\n56:   //\\n57:   // The filter is responsible to continue the stream by providing a body through calling\\n58:   // injectDecodedDataToFilterChain()/injectEncodedDataToFilterChain(), possibly multiple times\\n59:   // if the body needs to be divided into several chunks. The filter may need to handle\\n60:   // watermark events when injecting a body, see:\\n61:   // https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/blob/main/source/docs/flow_control.md.\\n62:   //\\n63:   // The last call to inject data MUST have end_stream set to true to conclude the stream.\\n64:   // If the filter cannot provide a body the stream should be reset.\\n65:   //\\n66:   // Adding a body through calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData() then\\n67:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is currently NOT supported and causes an assert failure.\\n68:   //\\n69:   // Adding trailers in this scenario is currently NOT supported.\\n70:   //\\n71:   // The filter MUST NOT attempt to continue the stream without providing a body using\\n72:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding().\\n73:   //\\n74:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding a body in this case by calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData()\\n75:   // then continueDecoding()/continueEncoding(). To support this a new FilterManager::IterationState\\n76:   // needs to be added and set when a filter returns this status in\\n77:   // FilterManager::decodeHeaders/FilterManager::encodeHeaders()\\n78:   // Currently, when a filter returns this, the IterationState is Continue. This causes ASSERTs in\\n79:   // FilterManager::commonContinue() to fail when continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is called;\\n80:   // due to trying to continue iteration when the IterationState is already Continue.\\n81:   // In this case, a different ASSERT will be needed to make sure the filter does not try to\\n82:   // continue without adding a body first.\\n83:   //\\n84:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding trailers in this case by implementing new functions to inject\\n85:   // trailers, similar to the inject data functions.\\n86:   ContinueAndDontEndStream,\\n87:   // Do not iterate for headers as well as data and trailers for the current filter and the filters\\n88:   // following, and buffer body data for later dispatching. ContinueDecoding() MUST\\n89:   // be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n90:   //\\n91:   // Used when a filter wants to stop iteration on data and trailers while waiting for headers'\\n92:   // iteration to resume.\\n93:   //\\n94:   // If buffering the request causes buffered data to exceed the configured buffer limit, a 413 will\\n95:   // be sent to the user. On the response path exceeding buffer limits will result in a 500.\\n96:   //\\n97:   // TODO(soya3129): stop metadata parsing when StopAllIterationAndBuffer is set.\\n98:   StopAllIterationAndBuffer,\\n99:   // Do not iterate for headers as well as data and trailers for the current filter and the filters\\n100:   // following, and buffer body data for later dispatching. continueDecoding() MUST\\n101:   // be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n102:   //\\n103:   // Used when a filter wants to stop iteration on data and trailers while waiting for headers'\\n104:   // iteration to resume.\\n105:   //\\n106:   // This will cause the flow of incoming data to cease until continueDecoding() function is called.\\n107:   //\\n108:   // TODO(soya3129): stop metadata parsing when StopAllIterationAndWatermark is set.\\n109:   StopAllIterationAndWatermark,\\n110: };\\n111: \\n112: /**\\n113:  * Return codes for encode on informative headers filter invocations.\\n114:  */\\n115: enum class Filter1xxHeadersStatus {\\n116:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\\n117:   Continue,\\n118:   // Do not iterate for informative headers on any of the remaining filters in the chain.\\n119:   //\\n120:   // Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from encodeData() or calling\\n121:   // continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n122:   StopIteration\\n123: };\\n124: \\n125: /**\\n126:  * Return codes for encode/decode data filter invocations. The connection manager bases further\\n127:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\\n128:  */\\n129: enum class FilterDataStatus {\\n130:   // Continue filter chain iteration. If headers have not yet been sent to the next filter, they\\n131:   // will be sent first via decodeHeaders()/encodeHeaders(). If data has previously been buffered,\\n132:   // the data in this callback will be added to the buffer before the entirety is sent to the next\\n133:   // filter.\\n134:   Continue,\\n135:   // Do not iterate to any of the remaining filters in the chain, and buffer body data for later\\n136:   // dispatching. Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\\n137:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n138:   //\\n139:   // This should be called by filters which must parse a larger block of the incoming data before\\n140:   // continuing processing and so can not push back on streaming data via watermarks.\\n141:   //\\n142:   // If buffering the request causes buffered data to exceed the configured buffer limit, a 413 will\\n143:   // be sent to the user. On the response path exceeding buffer limits will result in a 500.\\n144:   StopIterationAndBuffer,\\n145:   // Do not iterate to any of the remaining filters in the chain, and buffer body data for later\\n146:   // dispatching. Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\\n147:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n148:   //\\n149:   // This will cause the flow of incoming data to cease until one of the continue.*() functions is\\n150:   // called.\\n151:   //\\n152:   // This should be returned by filters which can nominally stream data but have a transient back-up\\n153:   // such as the configured delay of the fault filter, or if the router filter is still fetching an\\n154:   // upstream connection.\\n155:   StopIterationAndWatermark,\\n156:   // Do not iterate to any of the remaining filters in the chain, but do not buffer any of the\\n157:   // body data for later dispatching. A local reply can be\\n163:   // triggered via sendLocalReply() or encodeHeaders().\\n164:   StopIterationNoBuffer\\n165: };\\n166: \\n167: /**\\n168:  * Return codes for encode/decode trailers filter invocations. This method is used in\\n615:    * advanced cases in which a filter needs full control over how subsequent filters view data,\\n616:    * and does not want to make use of HTTP connection manager buffering. Using this method allows\\n617:    * a filter to buffer data (or not) and then periodically inject data to subsequent filters,\\n618:    * indicating end_stream at an appropriate time. namespace Http {\n33: \n34: /**\n35:  * Return codes for encode/decode headers filter invocations. The connection manager bases further\n36:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\n37:  */\n38: enum class FilterHeadersStatus {\n39:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\n40:   Continue,\n41:   // Do not iterate for headers on any of the remaining filters in the chain.\n42:   //\n43:   // Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\n44:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\n45:   //\n46:   // Note that if a local reply was sent, no further iteration for headers as well as data and\n47:   // trailers for the current filter and the filters following will happen. A local reply can be\n48:   // triggered via sendLocalReply() or encodeHeaders().\n49:   StopIteration,\n50:   // Continue headers iteration to remaining filters, but delay ending the stream. This status MUST\n51:   // NOT be returned when end_stream is already set to false.\n52:   //\n53:   // Used when a filter wants to add a body to a headers-only request/response, but this body is not\n54:   // readily available. Delaying end_stream allows the filter to add the body once it's available\n55:   // without stopping headers iteration.\n56:   //\n57:   // The filter is responsible to continue the stream by providing a body through calling\n58:   // injectDecodedDataToFilterChain()/injectEncodedDataToFilterChain(), possibly multiple times\n59:   // if the body needs to be divided into several chunks. The filter may need to handle\n60:   // watermark events when injecting a body, see:\n61:   // https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/blob/main/source/docs/flow_control.md.\n62:   //\n63:   // The last call to inject data MUST have end_stream set to true to conclude the stream.\n64:   // If the filter cannot provide a body the stream should be reset.\n65:   //\n66:   // Adding a body through calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData() then\n67:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is currently NOT supported and causes an assert failure.\n68:   //\n69:   // Adding trailers in this scenario is currently NOT supported.\n70:   //\n71:   // The filter MUST NOT attempt to continue the stream without providing a body using\n72:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding().\n73:   //\n74:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding a body in this case by calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData()\n75:   // then continueDecoding()/continueEncoding(). To support this a new FilterManager::IterationState\n76:   // needs to be added and set when a filter returns this status in\n77:   // FilterManager::decodeHeaders/FilterManager::encodeHeaders()\n78:   // Currently, when a filter returns this, the IterationState is Continue. This causes ASSERTs in\n79:   // FilterManager::commonContinue() to fail when continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is called;\n80:   // due to trying to continue iteration when the IterationState is already Continue.\n81:   // In this case, a different ASSERT will be needed to make sure the filter does not try to\n82:   // continue without adding a body first.\n83:   //\n84:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding trailers in this case by implementing new functions to inject\n85:   // trailers, similar to the inject data functions.\n86:   ContinueAndDontEndStream,\n87:   // Do not iterate for headers as well as data and trailers for the current filter and the filters\n88:   // following, and buffer body data for later dispatching. ContinueDecoding() MUST\n89:   // be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\n90:   //\n91:   // Used when a filter wants to stop iteration on data and trailers while waiting for headers'\n92:   // iteration to resume.\n93:   //\n94:   // If buffering the request causes buffered data to exceed the configured buffer limit, a 413 will\n95:   // be sent to the user. On the response path exceeding buffer limits will result in a 500.\n96:   //\n97:   // TODO(soya3129): stop metadata parsing when StopAllIterationAndBuffer is set.\n98:   StopAllIterationAndBuffer,\n99:   // Do not iterate for headers as well as data and trailers for the current filter and the filters\n100:   // following, and buffer body data for later dispatching. continueDecoding() MUST\n101:   // be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\n102:   //\n103:   // Used when a filter wants to stop iteration on data and trailers while waiting for headers'\n104:   // iteration to resume.\n105:   //\n106:   // This will cause the flow of incoming data to cease until continueDecoding() function is called.\n107:   //\n108:   // TODO(soya3129): stop metadata parsing when StopAllIterationAndWatermark is set.\n109:   StopAllIterationAndWatermark,\n110: };\n111: \n112: /**\n113:  * Return codes for encode on informative headers filter invocations.\n114:  */\n115: enum class Filter1xxHeadersStatus {\n116:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\n117:   Continue,\n118:   // Do not iterate for informative headers on any of the remaining filters in the chain.\n119:   //\n120:   // Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from encodeData() or calling\n121:   // continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\n122:   StopIteration\n123: };\n124: \n125: /**\n126:  * Return codes for encode/decode data filter invocations. The connection manager bases further\n127:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\n128:  */\n129: enum class FilterDataStatus {\n130:   // Continue filter chain iteration. If headers have not yet been sent to the next filter, they\n131:   // will be sent first via decodeHeaders()/encodeHeaders(). If data has previously been buffered,\n132:   // the data in this callback will be added to the buffer before the entirety is sent to the next\n133:   // filter.\n134:   Continue,\n135:   // Do not iterate to any of the remaining filters in the chain, and buffer body data for later\n136:   // dispatching. Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\n137:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\n138:   //\n139:   // This should be called by filters which must parse a larger block of the incoming data before\n140:   // continuing processing and so can not push back on streaming data via watermarks.\n141:   //\n142:   // If buffering the request causes buffered data to exceed the configured buffer limit, a 413 will\n143:   // be sent to the user. This avoids having\n1001:    * to deal with the existing buffered data and the data from the current callback.\n1002:    *\n1003:    * 3) If additional buffered body data needs to be added by a filter before continuation of data\n1004:    * to further filters (outside of callback context).\n1005:    *\n1006:    * 4) If additional data needs to be added in the encodeTrailers() callback, this method can be\n1007:    * called in the context of the callback. However if the iteration is stopped, the added data will\n1009:    * buffered, so that the further filters will not receive encodeData() before encodeHeaders().\n1010:    *\n1011:    * It is an error to call this method in any other case.\n1012:    *\n1013:    * See also injectEncodedDataToFilterChain() for a different way of passing data to further\n1014:    * filters and also how the two methods are different.\n1015:    *\n1016:    * @param data Buffer::Instance supplies the data to be encoded.\n1017:    * @param streaming_filter boolean supplies if this filter streams data or buffers the full body.\n1018:    */\n1019:   virtual void addEncodedData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool streaming_filter) PURE;\n1020: \n1021:   /**\n1022:    * Encode data directly to subsequent filters in the filter chain. This method is used in\n1023:    * advanced cases in which a filter needs full control over how subsequent filters view data,\n1024:    * and does not want to make use of HTTP connection manager buffering. Using this method allows\n1025:    * a filter to buffer data (or not) and then periodically inject data to subsequent filters,\n1026:    * indicating end_stream at an appropriate time. This can be used to implement rate limiting,\n1027:    * periodic data emission, etc.\n1028:    *\n1029:    * This method should only be called outside of callback context. I.e., do not call this method\n1030:    * from within a filter's encodeData() call.\n1031:    *\n1032:    * When using this callback, filters should generally only return\n1033:    * FilterDataStatus::StopIterationNoBuffer from their encodeData() call, since use of this method\n1034:    * indicates that a filter does not wish to participate in standard HTTP connection manager\n1035:    * buffering and continuation and will perform any necessary buffering and continuation on its\n1036:    * own.\n1037:    *\n1038:    * This callback is different from addEncodedData() in that the specified data and end_stream\n1039:    * status will be propagated directly to further filters in the filter chain. This is different\n1040:    * from addEncodedData() where data is added to the HTTP connection manager's buffered data with\n1041:    * the assumption that standard HTTP connection manager buffering and continuation are being used.\n1042:    */\n1043:   virtual void injectEncodedDataToFilterChain(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) PURE;\n1044: \n1045:   /**\n1046:    * Adds encoded trailers. May only be called in encodeData when end_stream is set to true.\n1047:    * If called in any other context, an assertion will be triggered.\n1048:    *\n1049:    * When called in encodeData, the trailers map will be initialized to an empty map and returned by\n1050:    * reference. Calling this function more than once is invalid.\n1051:    *\n1052:    * @return a reference to the newly created trailers map.\n1053:    */\n1054:   virtual ResponseTrailerMap& addEncodedTrailers() PURE;\n1055: \n1056:   /**\n1057:    * Attempts to create a locally generated response using the provided response_code and body_text\n1058:    * parameters. provided parameters.\n1061:    *\n1062:    * If a response has already started (e.g. if the router calls sendLocalReply after encoding\n1063:    * headers) this will either ship the reply directly to the downstream codec, or reset the stream.\n1064:    *\n1065:    * @param response_code supplies the HTTP response code.\n1066:    * @param body_text supplies the optional body text which is sent std::function<void(ResponseHeaderMap& headers)> modify_headers,\n1075:                               const absl::optional<Grpc::Status::GrpcStatus> grpc_status,\n1076:                               absl::string_view details) PURE;\n1077:   /**\n1078:    * Adds new metadata to be encoded.\n1079:    *\n1080:    * @param metadata_map supplies the unique_ptr of the metadata to be encoded.\n1081: virtual void onEncoderFilterAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark() PURE;\n1088: \n1089:   /**\n1090:    * Called when a encoder filter goes from over its high watermark to under its low watermark.\n1091:    */\n1092:   virtual void onEncoderFilterBelowWriteBufferLowWatermark() PURE;\n1093: \n1094:   /**\n1095:    * This routine may be called to change the buffer limit for encoder filters.\n1096: The filter factory pattern uses the FactoryBase template class from source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h, which inherits from CommonFactoryBase and NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory. Filters are registered using the REGISTER_FACTORY macro with the factory class and Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory base class. Examples of complete filter implementations were studied including: buffer filter (source/extensions/filters/http/buffer/), geoip filter (source/extensions/filters/http/geoip/), and health_check filter (source/extensions/filters/http/health_check/). Each filter follows the pattern of: (1) a filter class inheriting from Http::StreamDecoderFilter (or Http::StreamFilter for dual codec filters), (2) implementing all pure virtual methods from the interface, (3) a config factory class inheriting from Common::FactoryBase<ProtoType>, and (4) registration via REGISTER_FACTORY or LEGACY_REGISTER_FACTORY macros.
